 Sanskrit is the ancient language of India and hence it is respected but the teachers of Sanskrit are in bad shape
 aarthik tangi ke guzar rahe sanskrit shikshak kuch dinon se dilli main virodh pradarshan kar rahe hai
 On 27 December, these teachers started their demonstration at Jantar Mantar and then sat in front of Sanskrit Sansthan at Janakpuri
 dilli kii kadaake kii thand main yah log din-raat dharna die rahe lekin na to koi mantri inase milane aayaa na koi netaa
 At the swearing-in ceremony of the NDA government in 2014, many prominent leaders ranging from Sushma Swaraj, Uma Bharti, took oath in Sanskrit
 mukhya makasad tha sanskrit bhashaa or shiksha ko badhaava dena
 This initiative of the leaders was praised by many
 sirf shapath hi nahin, is sarkaar ke gathan ke baad kai aise nirnay liye gaye jo sanskrit bhashaa or shiksha kii badhaava dene ke liye hai
 Surprisingly, the salary of Sanskrit teachers working as guest and contract teachers is low and has not increased for many years
 pichley kuch dinon se dilli kii sadakon par sanskrit shikshak pradarshan kar rahe hai
 Teachers from different states of the country participated in this demonstration
 koi jammu-kashmir se aayaa he to koi kerala se
 Many women also participated in this performance
 mahilaon ko kahana he ki unhen meternity live bhi nahin milti he
 When no one came to meet them from the government and did not listen to their demand, on Monday, these teachers were seen begging on the streets of Delhi
 kai saalon se yah shikshak contract yaa guest ke rup main padhaa rahe hai
 The contract teachers get a salary of Rs 39 thousand while the guest teacher (guest teacher) gets Rs 25 thousand
 kai saalon se inkaa vetan nahin badha he
 These people are demanding regularization
